你是一个ETL专家, 正在查看如下ETL的定义(注意: 这里的所有节点都会运行在 Apache Spark 3.4上, 所有的SQL语法都是Spark的语法, 当用户让优化性能时, 不要给出建索引等通用的建议, 因为Spark不能建立索引, 并且这个ETL只能使用Spark SQL(不能使用DataFrame API), 主要给出可以"通过优化ETL节点的写法来优化性能"这种优化建议):

## 基本信息
- UniformResourceType: DATA_PROCESS_ETL

### 节点31
- Id: id_1665977264393

- Type: CALCULATOR
- **Sources (Inputs):**

- **Used By (Outputs):**
  - id_1665983493210 (新客/老客/散客占比)
- Position: (1200,1190)
- FormulaNames:
  - 新客/老客/散客
- 等价SQL:
```sql
SELECT
  *,
   
case when `会员编号` is null then "散客"
when `会员首购时间` >=TO_DATE(`m60_上市日期`)then "新客"
else "老客" end AS `新客/老客/散客`
FROM input1
```


### 节点32
- Id: id_1665983493210
- Name: 新客/老客/散客占比
- Type: SQL_SCRIPT
- **Sources (Inputs):**
  - id_1665977264393 (添加计算列)

- **Used By (Outputs):**
  - id_1665920481442 (关联数据)
- Position: (1390,1190)
- SqlScript:
```sql
SELECT input1.`商品款色SKC`,  
/*拼接整体新老散客*/
concat(case when sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`) = 0 then 0 else floor(round(sum(case when input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "新客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`),2)*100) end,"%","/",case when sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`) = 0 then 0 else floor(round(sum(case when input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "老客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`),2)*100) end,"%","/",case when sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`) = 0 then 0 else floor(round(sum(case when input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "散客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`),2)*100) end,"%") as `新客/老客/散客占比`, 
/*拼接各渠道新老散客*/
 concat(  
      "整体：",  
     	  concat(case when sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`) = 0 then 0 else floor(round(sum(case when input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "新客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`),2)*100) end,"%","/",case when sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`) = 0 then 0 else floor(round(sum(case when input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "老客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`),2)*100) end,"%","/",case when sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`) = 0 then 0 else floor(round(sum(case when input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "散客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(input1.`商品数量_排除赠品`),2)*100) end,"%"),
       char(10),
      "自营：",
 	      concat( case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "自营" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else 
             floor(round(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "自营" and input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "新客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "自营" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end),2)*100) end,"%","/",  
  	case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "自营" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else 
             floor(round(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "自营" and input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "老客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "自营" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end),2)*100) end,"%","/",  
   case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "自营" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else 
             floor(round(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "自营" and input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "散客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "自营" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end),2)*100) end,"%" ), 
      char(10), 
      "托管：",  
     	 concat( case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "托管（特许）" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else 
             floor(round(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "托管（特许）" and input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "新客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "托管（特许）" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end),2)*100) end,"%","/",  
  	case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "托管（特许）" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else 
             floor(round(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "托管（特许）" and input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "老客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "托管（特许）" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end),2)*100) end,"%","/",  
   case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "托管（特许）" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else 
             floor(round(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "托管（特许）" and input1.`新客/老客/散客` = "散客" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "托管（特许）" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end),2)*100) end,"%" ), 
     	char(10), 
     "电商：",  
     	concat( case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" then input1.`商品数量_排除赠品` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else
```

- Id: id_1737257123501
- Name: 添加计算列
- Type: CALCULATOR
- **Sources (Inputs):**

  - id_1671077307515 (选择列)
- Position: (290,1026)
- FormulaNames:
  - 大渠道-Z
- 等价SQL:
```sql
SELECT
  *,
  case 
when `库位编号` = "2000_3010" then "港澳" 
else `大渠道` end AS `大渠道-Z`
FROM input1
```

### 节点37
- Id: id_1665908781467
- Name: 添加计算列
- Type: CALCULATOR
- **Sources (Inputs):**
  - id_1719849211540 (SQL输入)

- **Used By (Outputs):**
  - id_1665911228530 (单款颜色销量)
  - id_1665911483824 (单款总销量)
  - id_1665842654202 (上周销量&累销)
  - id_1665910434035 (上周单款颜色销量)
  - id_1665910653479 (上周单款总销量)
  - id_1665913991011 (单款尺码数量)
  - id_1668246576871 (单款颜色尺码)
  - id_1672065778128 (单款颜色总销量)
- Position: (860,1030)
- FormulaNames:
  - 尺码(数值)
  - 初始化上市日期
  - 是否归为旧货
  - 上市2周
  - 上市4周
  - 上市8周
  - 上市16周
  - 期末周
- 等价SQL:
```sql
SELECT
  *,
  `尺码ID` AS `尺码(数值)`,
  case  
when `商品年` >= year(current_date()-1) then `实际上市日期`
when `商品年` = year(current_date()-1)-1 and `商品期` = "D期" and TO_DATE(CURRENT_DATE()-1) <=LAST_DAY(TO_DATE(concat(year(current_date()-1),"-03-01"))) then `实际上市日期`
else TO_DATE(CONCAT(year(current_date()-1),"-01-01")) 
end AS `初始化上市日期`,
  case  
when `商品年` >= year(current_date()-1) then "N"
when `商品年` = year(current_date()-1)-1 and `商品期` = "D期" and TO_DATE(CURRENT_DATE()-1) <=LAST_DAY(TO_DATE(concat(year(current_date()-1),"-03-01"))) then "N"
else "Y" end AS `是否归为旧货`,
   date_add(`上市日期_周初`,13)  AS `上市2周`,
   date_add(`上市日期_周初`,27)   AS `上市4周`,
   date_add(`上市日期_周初`,55)   AS `上市8周`,
   date_add(`上市日期_周初`,111)  AS `上市16周`,
   date_add(`上市日期_周初`,139)   AS `期末周`
FROM input1
```

```sql
from input1

order by input1.`skc编码`,`累计销量` desc
```

```sql
        floor(case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）"  and input1.`Z-统计日期` <= input1.`上市2周` then input1.`商品数量`*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)*100 end),"%","/", 
        floor(case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）"  and input1.`Z-统计日期` <= input1.`上市4周` then input1.`商品数量`*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)*100 end),"%","/", 
        floor(case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）"  and input1.`Z-统计日期` <= input1.`上市8周` then input1.`商品数量`*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)*100 end),"%","/",  
    	floor(case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）"  and input1.`Z-统计日期` <= input1.`上市16周` then input1.`商品数量`*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)*100 end),"%","/",
        floor(case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）"  and input1.`Z-统计日期` <= input1.`期末周` then input1.`商品数量`*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="托管（特许）" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)*100 end),"%"
      ) as `托管2/4/8/季末消化率(颜色)` ,
/*电商2/4/8/16/季末消化率*/ 
concat(
       floor(case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商"  and input1.`Z-统计日期` <= input1.`上市2周` then input1.`商品数量`*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)*100 end),"%","/", 
    	floor(case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商"  and input1.`Z-统计日期` <= input1.`上市4周` then input1.`商品数量`*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)*100 end),"%","/",  
    	floor(case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商"  and input1.`Z-统计日期` <= input1.`上市8周` then input1.`商品数量`*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)*100 end),"%","/", 
    	floor(case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商"  and input1.`Z-统计日期` <= input1.`上市16周` then input1.`商品数量`*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)*100 end),"%","/",
    	floor(case when sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end) = 0 then 0 else sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商"  and input1.`Z-统计日期` <= input1.`期末周` then input1.`商品数量`*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)/sum(case when input1.`大渠道`="电商" then (input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)*input1.`吊牌价` else 0 end)*100 end),"%"
      ) as `电商2/4/8/季末消化率(颜色)`
from input1 
GROUP by input1.`skc编码`
order by input1.`skc编码`,`累计销量` desc
```


### 节点39
- Id: id_1665911483824
- Name: 单款总销量
- Type: SQL_SCRIPT
- **Sources (Inputs):**
  - id_1665908781467 (添加计算列)

- **Used By (Outputs):**
  - id_1665911576635 (关联数据)
  - id_1665914930873 (关联数据)
  - id_1668248064549 (关联数据)
- Position: (1080,550)
- SqlScript:
```sql
SELECT input1.`skc编码`, 
floor(sum(input1.`商品数量` )) as `单款总销量` ,
floor(sum(input1.`期末库存数`)) as `单款总库存`, 
floor(sum(input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量`)) as `单款订单量`
from input1 
GROUP by input1.`skc编码`
```

```sql
replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(g) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `托管2/4/8/季末销量(颜色)`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(h) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `电商2/4/8/季末销量(颜色)`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(i) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `自营2/4/8/季末消化率(颜色)`,

from (
select *, 
    concat(floor(a.`累计销量`),"/",case when a.`单款总销量`=0 then 0 else floor(a.`累计销量`/a.`单款总销量`*100) end,"%","/",floor(a.`库存`),"/",case when a.`单款总库存`=0 then 0 else floor(a.`库存`/a.`单款总库存`*100) end,"%",char(10)) as a, 
    concat(a.`累计销量`," ",a.`自营/托管/电商颜色累计销量`,char(10)) as b,

    concat(a.`2/4/8/季末销量(颜色)`,char(10)) as e,

   	concat(a.`自营2/4/8/季末消化率(颜色)`,char(10)) as i, 
    concat(a.`托管2/4/8/季末消化率(颜色)`,char(10)) as j,

   	concat(floor(a.`库存`+a.`累计销量`)," ",a.`自营/托管/电商/总仓颜色总订单量`,char(10)) as m
   	
from (
SELECT * from input1  
  order by input1.`skc编码`,input1.`累计销量` desc
```

### 节点42
- Id: id_1665842654202
- Name: 上周销量&累销
- Type: SQL_SCRIPT
- **Sources (Inputs):**
  - id_1665908781467 (添加计算列)

- **Used By (Outputs):**
  - id_1665920481442 (关联数据)
- Position: (1080,160)
- SqlScript:
```sql
/*
线下渠道区域的顺序为华北/华东/华南/西南/北区/东区/南区；当前别名未改，顺序已调整，故需留意卡片上的别名需变更

*/

SELECT input1.`skc编码`,input1.`商品图片url`,input1.`颜色中文名称`,input1.`商品年`,input1.`实际波段`,input1.`运营波段（skc）`,input1.`实际上市日期`,input1.`初始化上市日期`,input1.`运营大类`,input1.`运营中类`,input1.`运营小类`,input1.`吊牌价`,input1.`吊牌价_港元`,input1.`销售折扣`, input1.`denim fit-family`,input1.`denim fit-name`,input1.`产品线(新)`,input1.`运营系列(新)`,input1.`版型`,input1.`是否归为旧货`,
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `上周销量`,  
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `上上周销量`,
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end)) as `上周销额`,  
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end)) as `上上周销额`,   
floor(sum(input1.`近14天销售数量`)) as `近14天销量`, 
floor(sum(input1.`近7天销售数量`)) as `近7天销量`, 
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,15) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `近15天销量`,
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,30) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `近30天销量`,
  
floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）","港澳") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end)) as `线下上周销额`, floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("电商") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end)) as `线上上周销额`,  
floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）","港澳") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end)) as `线下上上周销额`, 
floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("电商") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end)) as `线上上上周销额`,  
floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）","港澳") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `线下上周销量`, 
floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("电商") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `线上上周销量`, 
floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）","港澳") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `线下上上周销量`,

floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）","电商","港澳","总仓") then input1.`期末库存数`+input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `订单量`,

      floor(sum(case when input1.`区域` = "南区" then input1.`期末库存数` else 0 end))

    case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "A+" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "A+" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "A+" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end,"/",case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "A" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "A" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "A" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end, 
    char(10), 
    "B+/B/B-：", 
    case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B+" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "B+" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B+" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end,"/",case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "B" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end,"/",case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B-" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "B-" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B-" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end, 
    char(10), 
     "C+/C/C-：", 
    case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "C+" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "C+" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "C+" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end,"/",case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "C" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "C" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "C" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end,"/",case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "C-" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "C-" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "C-" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end, 
    char(10), 
    case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "O" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "O" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "O" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end
) as `店铺等级店均销量(线下)` 
*/ 

/*初始化消化率- - - - - - 主要用于初始化畅销款的判断*/ 
COALESCE(SUM(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_TRUNC('month',input1.`初始化上市日期`) and TO_DATE(current_date()-1) then input1.`吊牌价总额`  else 0 end)/SUM(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_TRUNC('month',input1.`初始化上市日期`) and TO_DATE(current_date()-1) then input1.`吊牌价总额`+input1.`期末库存吊牌额`  else 0 end),0) as `初始化消化率`,

/*电商平台*/
CONCAT_WS(
char(10),
concat("总：",floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))),
concat(
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "天猫"  and input1.`品牌` = "正价场" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)),"/",
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "抖音" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)),"/",
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "微信" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))
  ),
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`微分销门店编码` != "24251" and input1.`区域` not in ("抖音","微信") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))
) as `电商平台上周销量(天猫旗舰/抖音/微信<br>天猫奥莱/京东/小红书/得物<br>唯品会/员工特卖)`,

CONCAT_WS(
char(10),
concat("总：",floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)`else 0 end))),
concat(
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "天猫"  and input1.`品牌` = "正价场" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)`else 0 end)),"/",
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "抖音" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)`else 0 end)),"/",
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "微信" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)`else 0 end))
  ),
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`微分销门店编码` != "24251" and input1.`区域` not in ("抖音","微信") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)`else 0 end))
) as `电商平台上周销额(天猫旗舰/抖音/微信<br>天猫奥莱/京东/小红书/得物<br>唯品会/员工特卖)`,

CONCAT_WS(
char(10),
concat("总：",floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))),
concat(
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "天猫"  and input1.`品牌` = "正价场"  then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)),"/",
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "抖音"  then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)),"/",
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "微信"  then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))
  ),
        floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`微分销门店编码` != "24251" and input1.`区域` not in ("抖音","微信") then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))

) as `电商平台累计销量(天猫旗舰/抖音/微信<br>天猫奥莱/京东/小红书/得物<br>唯品会/员工特卖)`,

CONCAT_WS(
char(10),
concat("总：",FORMAT_NUMBER(ROUND(COALESCE(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))-1,0)*100,0),'#,###') || "%"),
  
concat(
        FORMAT_NUMBER(ROUND(COALESCE(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "天猫"  and input1.`品牌` = "正价场" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "天猫"  and input1.`品牌` = "正价场" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))-1,0)*100,0),'#,###') || "%","/",
        FORMAT_NUMBER(ROUND(COALESCE(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "抖音" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "抖音" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))-1,0)*100,0),'#,###') || "%","/",
        FORMAT_NUMBER(ROUND(COALESCE(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "微信" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "微信" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))-1,0)*100,0),'#,###') || "%"
  ),

        FORMAT_NUMBER(ROUND(COALESCE(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商"and input1.`微分销门店编码` != "24251" and input1.`区域` not in ("抖音","微信") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "天猫"  and input1.`品牌` = "奥莱" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))-1,0)*100,0),'#,###') || "%"

) as `电商平台上周销量环比(天猫旗舰/抖音/微信<br>天猫奥莱/京东/小红书/得物<br>唯品会/员工特卖)`,

CONCAT_WS(
char(10),
concat("总：",FORMAT_NUMBER(ROUND(COALESCE(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end))/floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end))-1,0)*100,0),'#,###') || "%"),
  
concat(
        FORMAT_NUMBER(ROUND(COALESCE(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "天猫"  and input1.`品牌` = "正价场" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end))/floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "天猫"  and input1.`品牌` = "正价场" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end))-1,0)*100,0),'#,###') || "%","/",
        FORMAT_NUMBER(ROUND(COALESCE(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "抖音" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end))/floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "抖音" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end))-1,0)*100,0),'#,###') || "%","/",
        FORMAT_NUMBER(ROUND(COALESCE(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "微信" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end))/floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "微信" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end))-1,0)*100,0),'#,###') || "%"
  ),

        FORMAT_NUMBER(ROUND(COALESCE(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`微分销门店编码` != "24251" and input1.`区域` not in ("抖音","微信") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end))/floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` = "电商" and input1.`区域`  = "天猫"  and input1.`品牌` = "奥莱" and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end))-1,0)*100,0),'#,###') || "%"
) as `电商平台上周销额环比(天猫旗舰/抖音/微信<br>天猫奥莱/京东/小红书/得物<br>唯品会/员工特卖)`

from input1 
GROUP by input1.`skc编码`,input1.`商品图片url`,input1.`颜色中文名称`,input1.`商品年`,input1.`实际波段`,input1.`运营波段（skc）`,input1.`实际上市日期`,input1.`初始化上市日期`,input1.`运营大类`,input1.`运营中类`,input1.`运营小类`,input1.`吊牌价`,input1.`吊牌价_港元`,input1.`销售折扣`,input1.`denim fit-family`,input1.`denim fit-name`,input1.`产品线(新)`,input1.`运营系列(新)`,input1.`版型`,input1.`是否归为旧货`
```
- 等价SQL:
```sql
/*
线下渠道区域的顺序为华北/华东/华南/西南/北区/东区/南区；当前别名未改，顺序已调整，故需留意卡片上的别名需变更

*/

SELECT input1.`skc编码`,input1.`商品图片url`,input1.`颜色中文名称`,input1.`商品年`,input1.`实际波段`,input1.`运营波段（skc）`,input1.`实际上市日期`,input1.`初始化上市日期`,input1.`运营大类`,input1.`运营中类`,input1.`运营小类`,input1.`吊牌价`,input1.`吊牌价_港元`,input1.`销售折扣`, input1.`denim fit-family`,input1.`denim fit-name`,input1.`产品线(新)`,input1.`运营系列(新)`,input1.`版型`,input1.`是否归为旧货`,
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `上周销量`,  
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `上上周销量`,
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end)) as `上周销额`,  
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,14) and DATE_SUB(current_date,8) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end)) as `上上周销额`,   
floor(sum(input1.`近14天销售数量`)) as `近14天销量`, 
floor(sum(input1.`近7天销售数量`)) as `近7天销量`, 
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,15) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `近15天销量`,
floor(sum(case when input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,30) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end)) as `近30天销量`,
  
floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）","港澳") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end)) as `线下上周销额`, floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("电商") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and DATE_SUB(current_date,1) then input1.`实际成交额(扣券)` else 0 end)) as `线上上周销额`,

    floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`Z-统计日期` BETWEEN DATE_SUB(current_date,7) and current_date()-weekday(current_date())-1 and input1.`店铺等级` = "O" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))
) as `店铺等级上周销量(线下)`, 
/*店铺等级累计销量(线下)*/

    "A+/A：",

    char(10), 
    "B+/B/B-：",

    char(10), 
     "C+/C/C-：",

    char(10), 
    floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "O" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))
) as `店铺等级累计销量(线下)`, 
/*店铺等级店均销量(线下)*/  
concat(  
    "A+/A：",  
    case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "A+" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "A+" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "A+" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end,"/",case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "A" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "A" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "A" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end, 
    char(10), 
    "B+/B/B-：", 
    case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B+" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "B+" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B+" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end,"/",case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "B" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end,"/",case when (COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B-" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1) = 0 then 0 else floor(floor(sum(case when input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") and input1.`店铺等级` = "B-" then input1.`商品数量` else 0 end))/(COUNT(DISTINCT case when input1.`店铺等级` = "B-" and input1.`大渠道` in ("自营","微营销","托管（特许）") then input1.`微分销门店编码` else 0 end)-1)) end,
```

- Id: id_1665910917974
- Name: 上周颜色销量占比合并
- Type: SQL_SCRIPT
- **Sources (Inputs):**
  - id_1665910790784 (关联数据)

- **Used By (Outputs):**
  - id_1665920481442 (关联数据)

- SqlScript:
```sql
select a.`skc编码`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(a) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `颜色/上周销量/%`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(b) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `颜色/上周销量`
from (
select *,concat(floor(a.`上周销量`),"/",case when a.`上周单款总销量`=0 then 0 else floor(round(a.`上周销量`/a.`上周单款总销量`,2)*100) end,"%",char(10)) as a, 
      concat(a.`上周销量`," ",a.`自营/托管/电商上周颜色销量`,char(10)) as b
from (
SELECT * from input1  
  order by input1.`skc编码`,input1.`上周销量` desc
 )a 
 )a 
 group by a.`skc编码`
```

```sql
from (

 )a

 group by a.`skc编码`
```

```sql
 group by a.`skc编码`
```

### 节点53
- Id: id_1668303966613

- Type: SQL_SCRIPT

- SqlScript:
```sql
select a.`skc编码`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(a) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `尺码订单`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(b) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `尺码订单%`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(c) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `尺码销售`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(d) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `尺码销售%`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(e) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `尺码库存`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(f) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `尺码库存%`, 
replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(g) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `颜色/尺码/订单量/订单量%/销量/销量%/库存/库存%`,replace(replace(replace(cast(collect_list(h) as string),'[',''),']',''),',','') as `尺码销售%(V2)`
from (
select *,
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",floor(a.`单款颜色尺码订单量`),";") as a, 
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",case when a.`单款颜色订单量`=0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码订单量`/a.`单款颜色订单量`,2)*100) end,"%",";") as b,  
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",floor(a.`单款颜色尺码累计销量`),";") as c,  
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",case when a.`单款颜色总销量`=0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码累计销量`/a.`单款颜色总销量`,2)*100) end,"%",";") as d, 
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",floor(a.`单款颜色尺码库存`),";") as e, 
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",case when a.`单款颜色总库存`=0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码库存`/a.`单款颜色总库存`,2)*100) end,"%",";") as f, 
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`,"/",a.`单款颜色尺码订单量`,"/",case when a.`单款颜色订单量`= 0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码订单量`/a.`单款颜色订单量`,2)*100) end,"%","/",a.`单款颜色尺码累计销量`,"/",case when a.`单款颜色总销量`= 0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码累计销量`/a.`单款颜色总销量`,2)*100) end,"%","/",a.`单款颜色尺码库存`,"/",case when a.`单款颜色总库存`= 0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码库存`/a.`单款颜色总库存`,2)*100) end,"%",";") as g , 
concat(a.`尺码ID`,"：",case when a.`单款颜色总销量`=0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码累计销量`/a.`单款颜色总销量`,2)*100) end,"%",char(10)) as h
from (
SELECT * from input1  
  order by input1.`skc编码`,input1.`尺码(数值)` asc
 )a 
 )a 
 group by a.`skc编码`
```

```sql
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",case when a.`单款颜色订单量`=0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码订单量`/a.`单款颜色订单量`,2)*100) end,"%",";") as b,  
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",floor(a.`单款颜色尺码累计销量`),";") as c,  
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",case when a.`单款颜色总销量`=0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码累计销量`/a.`单款颜色总销量`,2)*100) end,"%",";") as d, 
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",floor(a.`单款颜色尺码库存`),";") as e, 
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`," ",case when a.`单款颜色总库存`=0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码库存`/a.`单款颜色总库存`,2)*100) end,"%",";") as f, 
concat(a.`尺码中文描述`,"/",a.`单款颜色尺码订单量`,"/",case when a.`单款颜色订单量`= 0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码订单量`/a.`单款颜色订单量`,2)*100) end,"%","/",a.`单款颜色尺码累计销量`,"/",case when a.`单款颜色总销量`= 0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码累计销量`/a.`单款颜色总销量`,2)*100) end,"%","/",a.`单款颜色尺码库存`,"/",case when a.`单款颜色总库存`= 0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码库存`/a.`单款颜色总库存`,2)*100) end,"%",";") as g , 
concat(a.`尺码ID`,"：",case when a.`单款颜色总销量`=0 then 0 else floor(ROUND(a.`单款颜色尺码累计销量`/a.`单款颜色总销量`,2)*100) end,"%",char(10)) as h
from (
SELECT * from input1  
  order by input1.`skc编码`,input1.`尺码(数值)` asc
 )a 
 )a 
 group by a.`skc编码`
```

### 节点72
- Id: id_1714895024859
- Name: 添加计算列
- Type: CALCULATOR
- **Sources (Inputs):**
  - id_1679104233068 (关联数据)

- **Used By (Outputs):**
  - id_1714899392166 (添加计算列)
- Position: (2280,230)
- FormulaNames:
  - 初始化上市周
- 等价SQL:
```sql
SELECT
  *,
  case 
when `商品年` >= year(current_date()-1) then DATEDIFF(current_date()-1,TO_DATE(`初始化上市日期`)) div 7 + 1
when `商品年` = year(current_date()-1)-1 and `商品期` = "D期" and TO_DATE(CURRENT_DATE()-1) <=LAST_DAY(TO_DATE(concat(year(current_date()-1),"-03-01"))) then DATEDIFF(current_date()-1,TO_DATE(`初始化上市日期`)) div 7 + 1
else DATEDIFF(current_date()-1,`初始化上市日期`) div 7 +1 end
 AS `初始化上市周`
FROM input1
```

### 节点75
- Id: id_1679109200466
- Name: 消化率落差
- Type: CALCULATOR
- **Sources (Inputs):**
  - id_1679110531497 (Null值替换)

- **Used By (Outputs):**
  - id_1678719893273 (单品图册(SKC版))
- Position: (2610,230)
- FormulaNames:
  - 全渠道消化率落差
  - 全渠道畅平销
  - spu
- 等价SQL:
```sql
SELECT
  *,
  `初始化消化率`-`全渠道消化率目标` AS `全渠道消化率落差`,
  case 
when `是否归为旧货` = "Y" and `初始化消化率` > `全渠道消化率目标`*1.2 then "畅销"
when `是否归为旧货` = "Y" and `初始化消化率`  between `全渠道消化率目标`*0.8 and `全渠道消化率目标`*1.2 then "平销"
when `是否归为旧货` = "Y" and `初始化消化率` < `全渠道消化率目标`*0.8  then "滞销"
when `初始化上市周` = 1 and `初始化消化率`-`全渠道消化率目标` >= -0.02 then "畅销"   
when `初始化上市周` = 1 and `初始化消化率`-`全渠道消化率目标` >= -0.16 and `初始化消化率`-`全渠道消化率目标` < -0.02 then "平销"  
when `初始化上市周` = 1 and `初始化消化率`-`全渠道消化率目标` < -0.16 then "滞销" 
when `初始化上市周` between 2 and 8 and `初始化消化率`-`全渠道消化率目标` >= -0.05 then "畅销" 
when `初始化上市周` between 2 and 8 and `初始化消化率`-`全渠道消化率目标` >= -0.16 and `初始化消化率`-`全渠道消化率目标` < -0.05 then "平销" 
when `初始化上市周` between 2 and 8 and `初始化消化率`-`全渠道消化率目标` < -0.16 then "滞销" 
when `初始化上市周` > 8 and `初始化消化率`-`全渠道消化率目标` >=0 then "畅销"  
when `初始化上市周` > 8 and `初始化消化率` between `全渠道消化率目标`*0.8 and `全渠道消化率目标`*0.9999 then "平销"
when `初始化上市周` > 8 and `初始化消化率` < `全渠道消化率目标`*0.8 then "滞销" 
else null end

 AS `全渠道畅平销`,
  case 
when `商品年` < 2025 then SUBSTR(`skc编码`,1,12)
else SUBSTR(`skc编码`,1,10)end AS `spu`
FROM input1
```
